document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);\n    return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Debounced search function\n  const debouncedSearch = useCallback((searchQuery: string) => {\n    setIsLoading(true);\n    \n    // Simulate API delay\n    setTimeout(() => {\n      const searchResults = searchInData(searchQuery);\n      const searchSuggestions = getSuggestions(searchQuery);\n      \n      setResults(searchResults);\n      setSuggestions(searchSuggestions);\n      setIsLoading(false);\n    }, 300);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Handle input change\n  const handleInputChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const value = e.target.value;\n    setQuery(value);\n    \n    if (value.trim()) {\n      debouncedSearch(value);\n    } else {\n      setResults([]);\n      setSuggestions([]);\n      setIsLoading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Handle input focus\n  const handleFocus = () => {\n    setIsOpen(true);\n  };\n\n  // Handle recent search click\n  const handleRecentSearchClick = (searchTerm: string) => {\n    setQuery(searchTerm);\n    debouncedSearch(searchTerm);\n    inputRef.current?.focus();\n  };\n\n  // Handle suggestion click\n  const handleSuggestionClick = (suggestion: SearchSuggestion) => {\n    setQuery(suggestion.text);\n renderExpandedRow,\n  selectable = false,\n  onSelectionChange,\n  className = '',\n}: TableProps<T>) {\n  const [sortConfig, setSortConfig] = useState<SortConfig<T>>(null);\n  const [filters, === 'asc' ? -1 : 1;\n        }\n        if (aValue > bValue) {\n          return sortConfig.direction === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;\n        }\n        return 0;\n      });\n    }\n\n    return filtered;\n  }, setExpandedRows(prev => {\n      const newSet = new Set(prev);\n      if (newSet.has(rowId)) {\n        newSet.delete(rowId);\n      } else {\n        newSet.add(rowId);\n      }\n      return (newSet.has(rowId)) {\n        newSet.delete(rowId);\n      } else {\n        newSet.add(rowId);\n      }\n      \n      // Notify parent of selection change\n      const selectedData = setGlobalFilter(e.target.value)}\n                className=\"pl-10\"\n              />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Selection Info */}\n          {selectable && selectedRows.size > 0 && (\n            <div className=\"text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400\">\n              {selectedRows.size} of {processedData.length} selected\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Column Filters */}\n        <div className=\"mt-4 grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4\">\n          {columns.filter(col => />\n              <Input\n                placeholder={`Filter by ${column.header.toLowerCase()}...`}\n                value={filters[column.id] || ''}\n                onChange={(e) => Table */}\n      <div className=\"overflow-x-auto\">\n        <table className=\"w-full\">\n          <thead className=\"bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-800\">\n            <tr>\n              {selectable && (\n                <th className=\"px-4 py-3 text-left\">\n                  <input\n                    type=\"checkbox\"\n                    checked={processedData.length > 0 && processedData.every(row => selectedRows.has(row.id))}\n                    onChange={toggleSelectAll}\n                    className=\"rounded border-gray-300 text-blue-600 focus:ring-blue-500\"\n                  />\n                </th>\n              )}\n              {expandable && <th className=\"px-4 py-3 w-8\"></th>}\n              {columns.map(column => (\n                <th \n
